id="bread-crumb" class="w1xblh6d"><img src="/assets/icons/breadCrumb/symbol-icon-home.svg" alt="home-icon" class="lp9mpbn"/><div class="btlhmn6"><a class="b17vyawb" href="/news/cat/tw_stock">台股</a><a class="b17vyawb" href="/news/cat/tw_stock_news">台股新聞</a></div></section><article class="mfxje1x"><section class="t1el8oye"><span class="bzubwch"> <!-- -->台股</span><h1>〈台股盤後〉台積電推高台股漲238點再刷新天價 周線連七漲噴漲3537點</h1></section><p class="alr4vq1"><span class="signature">鉅亨網記者吳承諦 台北</span><span class="separator"></span><time dateTime="2025-10-09T06:08:42.000Z">2025-10-09 14:08</time></p><main id="article-container" class="c1tt5pk2" style="--c1tt5pk2-0:20px"><section style="margin-top:30px"><p>台股今 (9) 日在台積電衝高帶動下，指數一度大漲 400 點，衝上 27463.12 點新高，終場漲點略為收斂至 238.24 點，以 27301.92 點作收，再度創下收盤新高，成交量 5643.3 億元。本周上漲 540.86 點，周線連續 7 周上漲共 3537 點，周 K 線連 2 紅。</p></section><p><div class="c1hvmcli"><figure><div class="iirgi4a"><img alt="cover image of news article" fetchPriority="high" decoding="async" data-nimg="fill" class="cr8g41v" style="position:absolute;height:100%;width:100%;left:0;top:0;right:0;bottom:0;color:transparent" src="https://cimg.cnyes.cool/prod/news/6183608/l/c5117adb4a5f1ec1c63a070452964381.jpg"/></div><figcaption class="c1gcnfq1">〈台股盤後〉台積電推高台股漲238點再刷新天價 周線連七漲3537點。(圖：shutterstock)</figcaption></figure></div></p><section style="margin-top:30px">

</section><section style="margin-top:30px"><p>電子權值股今天漲多於跌，市場期待台積電 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/2330" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:2330:STOCK:COMMON">2330-TW</a>) 下午 公布 9 月業績，盤中一度創下 1455 元新高，終場上漲 25&nbsp;元，漲逾 1%，來到 1440&nbsp;元；聯發科 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/2454" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:2454:STOCK:COMMON">2454-TW</a>) 上漲 10&nbsp;元，漲約 0.5%，來到 1345&nbsp;元；日月光投控 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/3711" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:3711:STOCK:COMMON">3711-TW</a>) 漲約 2%，聯電 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/2303" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:2303:STOCK:COMMON">2303-TW</a>) 漲約 1%，廣達 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/2382" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:2382:STOCK:COMMON">2382-TW</a>) 跌約 2%，鴻海 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/2317" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:2317:STOCK:COMMON">2317-TW</a>) 於平盤下方。</p></section><section>

</section><div id="div-gpt-ad-cnyes_news_article_middle_1" class="a1mzdm1v" style="--a1mzdm1v-0:728px;--a1mzdm1v-1:90px;--a1mzdm1v-2:728px;--a1mzdm1v-3:90px;--a1mzdm1v-4:32px;--a1mzdm1v-5:32px;--a1mzdm1v-6:auto;--a1mzdm1v-7:auto"><span aria-live="polite" aria-busy="true"><span class="react-loading-skeleton" style="border-radius:6px;width:100%;height:100%">‌</span><br/></span></div><section style="margin-top:30px"><p>DRAM 缺貨話題持續發酵，記憶體類股走強，宇瞻 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/8271" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:8271:STOCK:COMMON">8271-TW</a>) 漲停，凌航 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/3135" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWG:3135:STOCK:COMMON">3135-TW</a>)、南亞科 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/2408" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:2408:STOCK:COMMON">2408-TW</a>) 漲約 8%，華邦電 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/2344" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:2344:STOCK:COMMON">2344-TW</a>) 漲約 5%。</p></section><section style="margin-top:30px">

</section><section style="margin-top:30px"><p>台積電強攻帶動半導體股受資金追捧，封測、設備族群紛紛上攻，典範 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/3372" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:3372:STOCK:COMMON">3372-TW</a>)、華泰 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/2329" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:2329:STOCK:COMMON">2329-TW</a>) 強攻漲停，亞翔 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/6139" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:6139:STOCK:COMMON">6139-TW</a>) 漲約 8%，菱生 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/2369" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:2369:STOCK:COMMON">2369-TW</a>) 漲逾 4%。</p></section><section style="margin-top:30px">

</section><section style="margin-top:30px"><p>外資報告指出 ABF 載板及 BT 載板價格都上漲，且未來可能缺貨，帶動載板族群走強，景碩 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/3189" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:3189:STOCK:COMMON">3189-TW</a>) 亮紅燈，南電 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/8046" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:8046:STOCK:COMMON">8046-TW</a>) 漲近 2%，欣興 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/3037" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:3037:STOCK:COMMON">3037-TW</a>) 漲近 1%。</p></section><section style="margin-top:30px">
